text: "158 CHRISTIAN EXPERIENCE.\n237\n11s.\nKIRKHAM.\nPrecious Promises.\nOW firm a foundation, ye saints of the Lord,\nWhat more can he say than to you he hath said-\nYou who unto Jesus for refuge have fled?\n2 In every condition-in sickness, in health-\nIn poverty\'s vale, or abounding in wealth-\nAt home and abroad-on the land, on the sea-\n\"As thy days may demand, shall thy strength\never be.\nBA55\n3 \"Fear not: I am with thee: O be not dis-\nmay\'d!\nI, I am thy God, and will still give thee aid:\nI\'ll strengthen thee, help thee, and cause thee\nto stand,\nUpheld by my righteous, omnipotent hand.\n4 \"When through the deep waters I call thee\nto go,\nThe rivers of wo shall not thee overflow;\nFor I will be with thee, thy troubles to bless,\nAnd sanctify to thee thy deepest distress.\n5 \"When through fiery trials thy pathway\nshall lie,\nMy grace, all-sufficient, shall be thy supply:\nThe flame shall not hurt thee: I only design\nThy dross to consume, and thy gold to refine.\n6 \"E\'en down to old age, all my people shall\n<\nprove\nMy sovereign, eternal, unchangeable love;\nAnd when hoary hairs shall their temples adorn,\nLike lambs they shall still in my bosom be borne.\n7 \"The soul that on Jesus still leans for repose,\nI will not, I will not desert to his foes:\nThat soul, though all hell should endeavour te\nshake,\nI\'ll never, no never, NO NEVER forsake.\""
